<GmapID>0x80c2c0ec0d9543e3:0x7f5f575b3163561f< /GmapID><UserId.>113834920671509264977< /UserId.>< review>
Multiple rings to choose from, many great trainers, good facilities--clean bathrooms, changing areas, shower available, drink/snack machines, water fountains, tables and shade. Love the lit rings--can ride until 9/10pm if needed! Board is somewhat pricey compared to other facilities and the arena footings need improvement, but personally can't beat the proximity and location. Staff/personnel on-site 24/7. Definitely a little oasis.</review>

<Text>A&S Smog is definitely the bee's knees! My husband and I went first thing Monday morning to get our vehicle smogged. Its a small place but kept well maintained.  We were greeted by Tony, a very pleasant individual and honest. He right away took our vehicle into the garage and started his thing. I filled out one simple paperwork and in about 10 minutes we were done! Unfortunately our vehicle did not pass smog because it "wasn't ready". The amazing Tony explained to us why it did not pass. When replacing an O2 sensor, the vehicle needs to be driven for about 40-80 miles before the vehicle resets itself. Tony advised us to drive about 40 miles then come back. 40 miles later, we return to Tony and he checked with his reader before performing the second test. Sure enough, our vehicle was ready for the test (And to think, other places would have charged up the whoohaa just to do the same thing)... final verdict: PASSED with flying colors! < Review>
My favorite weekend coffee spot! Same great coffee and food as the other Old Soul locations. On the weekends its pretty much empty and there's tons of parking available on the side street. I haven't been here on a weekday when I would assume it's way busier due to the proximity to the Capitol and downtown office buildings. Love their mochas, tea selections and PB cookies, but everything is good. There is only one barista running register and making drinks, but it's never been crowded when I go, so service is still relatively quick.</Review>

Liana Haig</user_name>
<Time>1546391895472< /Time><rate>5< /rate>< Review>
My boyfriend and I both agree that this place has the best pizza we have ever had. I lived in NY for 8 years so I think I know if a pizza is good. The sauce is really flavorful and rich and there is a lot of cheese and the cheese tastes amazing! I've had too much pizza where  the cheese tastes like nothing and this place does not use that kind of cheap tasting  cheese. The crust is also so delicious, it makes you wanna eat the crust edges. I really like the feel of the restaurant, it feels Italian in there. They also have a big menu with many options besides pizza. The broasted chicken is really good, and the minestrone soup is amazing with fresh veggies and tasted so home made!
It's not a very cheap menu but it's so worth it because of the quality and the amount you get. We got a medium pizza and it lasted us 2 days eventhough my bf is a big eater.< /Review>

My boyfriend loves sandwiches, almost more than he loves me, and he loves The Gourmet Bagger. No doubt, when we are running around in Pt. Loma, he always suggests eating here. As someone who enjoys sandwiches, but doesn't want to eat them every day like he does, I must say the GB is still a delicious little hidden gem. They have a friendly staff, and they have some really yummy sandwiches. Great thing too, is you can modify any sandwich to you liking. They also have some really fresh bread and ingredients. Don't forget to order extra cookies. The cookies alone get their own star. Yum.</text>

1553206312872</time>
<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
Really tasty sandwiches. Their Philly was great, but oddly came with tomato and lettuce (hot lettuce is pretty gross imo), but I asked if I could take off these toppings and add hot peppers; then it was otherwise one of the best Phillys I've eaten. It looked small, but they did not skimp on the meat, simply opting for a smaller style of french roll--and after eating it--I actually now prefer it to the typical bready alternative.

tl;dr Every locally owned store has its quirks--this shop seems to prefer odd condiment combinations over traditional ones--pay attention to the ingredients on your sub, and revel in a delicious community-owned sandwich shop that tries new combinations; it doesn't always work, but the passion is addictive, much like their sandwiches.<//Text>

<rating>5< /rating>< text>
This nature center is open.. good spot to educate your children and yourself.
Can stop by and have lunch outside which has picnic tables under trees for shade.. outside are areas were live animal's are kept in captivity..Such as several turtles,red tail hawk,, owl,, racoons,,and other animals.. inside the museum are live Snakes such as King snakes, rat snakes gopher snake & a rosey boa snakes.also Tarantulas.. display of various taxidermied animals displayed throughout the museum.
Including a gift shop. The associates that work here have great attitudes and friendly..the bathrooms here are very well Maintained with tissues & soap for hygiene care.. the trails here are full of reptiles,,my advice were high laced boots cus there's Snakes around the whole nature center including rattle Snakes and other creatures that blend in with the terrains here throughout the trails . this nature center here @ Whittier Narrows is safe to visit even though homeless have been seen to gather in the trails...the El Monte Police pass through here on a regular basis which makes it more safe for visitors.. come check it out with the young ones,, I'm sure they'll be surprised to see the live animals & reptiles kept in captivity..pack a lunch with some refreshments and snacks for kids and spend a day here and the Whittier Narrows Recreation Area which is located across the street from the Whittier Narrows Nature center..
Enjoy and always be aware of your surroundings and be safe..</text>

<user_id>115870284657208684796</user_id><user_name>Mary Parker</user_name><date>1557671409990</date><Rating>2</Rating>< Review>
My husband & I went here for a quick bite to eat. They have an extensive menu that was very sticky as if it had old oil on it. We both chose the $10.95 lunch salad. With it we got a chicken breast or pc of tilapia. Plus there were small pcs of small servings of carrot cake, cheesecake, caramel pecan brownies, & a tray of great looking cookies.

We normally split a Coke cause I only drink a few sips. They brought what looked to me 2be a liter of Coke much too large for both of us. This tasted awful; I thought it was diet and sent it back. The 2nd 1 arrived and was equally bad. The syrup/soda water mix had 2b off or diet was in the regular Cole spot.

The salad bar itself was fair. Nothing special, but u could make a decent salad off of it. I love cantelope and pineapple chunks, they had both; pineapple was excellent! The cantelope looked great, had good texture, but tasted musty; I didn't eat my 3 pcs.

Next came our chicken for me and fish for my husband. He'll eat anything, I am the picky one. 1st I smelled his fish fr across the table. Then when I looked at my chicken, all I saw was a cooked pc of meat, with grease floating on top. Both appeared to have been grilled, but both had this layer of grease on them. I put a napkin on the chicken to blot up this liquid. I wound up covering it up & passing to my husband, cause it looked so bad, the smell of both was nauseating me. He only picked at his fish. I dont think he had 1 bite. He decided we'd take boith home to our 2 doxies.

We split the 3 desserts. They were all only slivers, perfect size for a salad bar. I liked the cheesecake. He loved the carrot cake, his fav cake. The brownie looked great, but that's all. It tasted as if it were missing something. Oh and the beautiful spread of cookies...not so  good either.

We pd & left, carrying our box of chicken & fish for our dogs. We drove to a shop in the same strip mall, went in a few minutes. When we returned & he opened my car door, I told him he had to put the chicken & fish in the trunk. The aroma was so over-powering, that my stomach turned, again. Instead, he picked the box up and threw it in a nearby trashcan, adding that he was bothered by the smell & it not being fit to feed our dogs.

I gave it 2 stars for the carrot cake & cheesecake slivers. They were just the right size for a taste. Plus they were good. Given the lacking brownie, I'd guess they weren't made in house.<//Review>
